  COLUMN DEFINITIONS:
  [1] Cloud-Only  : ALL tasks sent to cloud (no MOAOA, no offloading)

  [3] MOAOA-Dyn   : MOAOA with dynamic burst workload (stress test)

  NOTE: Cloud-Only baseline uses same delay/energy model as MOAOA
        for a fair apples-to-apples comparison.
  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
  Metric                            [1] Cloud-Only    [2] MOAOA-Static  [3] MOAOA-Dynamic
  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
  Total Tasks                       3372              3372              20              
  Task Compute Energy (J)           2529000.00        658980.00         5060.00         
    vs Cloud-Only                   baseline          ↓ 73.9           %  ↓ 71.9           %
  Total Delay (ms)                  16897.6339        3027.0286         23.4100         
    vs Cloud-Only                   baseline          ↓ 82.1           %  ↓ 83.8           %
  Avg Energy per Task (J)           750.0000          195.4270          253.0000        
  Avg Delay per Task (ms)           5.0112            0.8977            1.1705          
  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────
  Tasks → EDGE                      0 (all cloud)     2769              16              
  Tasks → FOG                       0 (all cloud)     595               4               
  Tasks → CLOUD                     3372              0                 0               
  Overloaded Rounds                 N/A               0                 0 / 3           
  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  INTERPRETATION
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════

  WHY MOAOA-STATIC BEATS CLOUD-ONLY:
  • Edge nodes: 0.4 J/MI vs Cloud: 1.5 J/MI  →  73% lower energy per task
  • Edge comm delay: data/10000 vs Cloud: data/100  →  100× faster comm
  • 2769 tasks kept at edge, 595 at fog — only 0 sent to cloud

  WHY MOAOA-DYNAMIC DEGRADES:
  • Burst arrivals exceed edge/fog capacity → overflow to cloud
  • Queuing delays accumulate at overloaded nodes
  • MOAOA requires re-optimization each round (150 iters × 100 pop)
    but burst tasks arrive faster than optimizer converges
  • 0 of 3 rounds experienced overload
  • This motivates adaptive/online algorithms (future work)
  ───────────────────────────────────────────────────

═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
  MOAOA Parameters Used (Ali et al. 2024, Table 8)
═══════════════════════════════════════════════════════
    Population Size                   : 100
    Max Iterations                    : 150
    Vmax                              : 0.9
    Vmin                              : 0.2
    Escalation (α)                    : 5.0
    Control Param (Cp)                : 0.5
    Weight (W)                        : 0.5 (equal priority: delay + energy)
    Edge Capacity                     : 2 tasks/node/round
    Fog Capacity                      : 6 tasks/node/round
    Cloud Capacity                    : Unbounded
